= 30  # Time threshold for loitering\nERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD = 0.7  # Movement variance threshold\nFPS = 10  # Processed frames per second\n\n# ---------------- MODEL LOADING ----------------\nprint(\"Loading YOLOv5 model...\")\nmodel = torch.hub.load('ultralytics/yolov5', 'custom', path=MODEL_PATH)\nmodel.conf = 0.4  # Confidence threshold\n\n# ---------------- TRACKING UTILS ----------------\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n        centroids = np.array([[(x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2] for x1, y1, x2, y2 in detections])\n        assigned = set()\n        updated_tracks = dict()\n        # Assign detections to existing tracks\n        for tid, track in self.tracks.items():\n            if len(track['centroids']) == 0:\n                continue\n            prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n            min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n            if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # Threshold\n                assigned.add(min_idx)\n                new_centroids = track['centroids']\n                new_centroids.append(centroids[min_idx])\n                updated_tracks[tid] = {'centroids': new_centroids, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        # New tracks\n        for i, c in enumerate(centroids):\n            if i not in assigned:\n                updated_tracks[self.next_id] = {'centroids': deque([c], maxlen=100), 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n                self.next_id += 1\n        # Remove lost tracks\n        self.tracks = {tid: tr for tid, tr in updated_tracks.items() if frame_idx - tr['last_seen'] < self.max_lost}\n        return self.tracks\n\n# ---------------- ANOMALY DETECTION ----------------\ndef detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time):\n    \"\"\"Detects people staying in same area for LOITERING_TIME_SEC.\"\"\"\n    loitering_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        if len(tr['centroids']) < FPS * LOITERING_TIME_SEC:\n            continue\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        spread = np.linalg.norm(positions - positions.mean(axis=0), axis=1)\n        if np.max(spread) < 40:  # 40 pixels radius\n            loitering_ids.append(tid)\n    return loitering_ids\n\ndef detect_erratic(tracks):\n    \"\"\"Detects erratic movement by high variance in direction.\"\"\"\n    erratic_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        if len(positions) < 10:\n            continue\n        diffs = np.diff(positions, axis=0)\n        angles = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n        variance = np.var(angles)\n        if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD:\n            erratic_ids.append(tid)\n    return erratic_ids\n\n# ---------------- ALERTING ----------------\ndef send_email_alert(subject, body):\n    msg = EmailMessage()\n    msg['Subject'] = subject\n    msg['From'] = EMAIL_SENDER\n    msg['To'] = ALERT_EMAIL\n    msg.set_content(body)\n    try:\n        with smtplib.SMTP(SMTP_SERVER, SMTP_PORT) as server:\n            server.starttls()\n            server.login(EMAIL_SENDER, EMAIL_PASSWORD)\n            server.send_message(msg)\n        print(f\"Email alert sent: {subject}\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Email alert failed: {e}\")\n\ndef send_push_alert(title, message):\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(PUSH_API_URL, render_template('dashboard.html')\n\n@app.route('/alerts')\ndef get_alerts():\n    return jsonify(list(alert_queue))\n\ndef gen_frames():\n    while True:\n        if frame_buffer:\n            frame = frame_buffer[-1]\n            ret, buffer = cv2.imencode('.jpg', frame)\n            frame_bytes = buffer.tobytes()\n            yield (b'--frame\\r\\n'\n                   b'Content-Type: image/jpeg\\r\\n\\r\\n' + frame_bytes + b'\\r\\n')\n        time.sleep(1/FPS)\n\n@app.route('/video_feed')\ndef video_feed():\n    return Response(gen_frames(), mimetype='multipart/x-mixed-replace; boundary=frame')\n\n# ---------------- MAIN INFERENCE LOOP ----------------\ndef surveillance_loop():\n    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(RTSP_URL)\n    tracker = SimpleTracker()\n    frame_idx = 0\n    start_time = time.time()\n    alert_sent_ids = set()\n    performance = {'frames': 0, 'detections': 0, 'alerts': 0, 'start': time.time()}\n    while True:\n        ret, frame = cap.read()\n        if not ret:\n            print(\"Failed to read frame. Reconnecting...\")\n            cap.release()\n            time.sleep(2)\n            cap = cv2.VideoCapture(RTSP_URL)\n            continue\n        frame_idx += 1\n        if frame_idx % int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FPS)//FPS) != 0:\n            continue  # Downsample FPS\n        results = model(frame)\n        detections = []\n        for *xyxy, conf, cls in results.xyxy[0].cpu().numpy():\n            if int(cls) == 0:  # person class in COCO\n                x1, y1, x2, y2 = map(int, xyxy)\n                detections.append((x1, y1, x2, y2))\n                cv2.rectangle(frame, (x1, y1), (x2, y2), (0,255,0), 2)\n        performance['frames'] += 1\n        performance['detections'] += len(detections)\n        tracks = tracker.update(detections, frame_idx)\n        # Draw tracks\n        for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n            c = tr['centroids'][-1]\n            cv2.putText(frame, f\"ID:{tid}\", (c[0], c[1]), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.5, (255,0,0), 2)\n        # Anomaly detection\n        loitering_ids = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_idx/FPS)\n        erratic_ids = detect_erratic(tracks)\n        for tid in loitering_ids:\n            if tid not in alert_sent_ids:\n                msg = f\"Loitering detected for ID {tid}\"\n                alert_queue.append({'type': 'loitering', 'id': tid, 'time': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')})\n                send_email_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                send_push_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                socketio.emit('alert', {'type': 'loitering', 'id': tid, 'msg': msg})\n                alert_sent_ids.add(tid)\n                performance['alerts'] += 1\n                cv2.putText(frame, \"LOITERING\", (c[0], c[1]-20), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.7, (0,0,255), 2)\n        for tid in erratic_ids:\n            if tid not in alert_sent_ids:\n                msg = f\"Erratic movement detected for ID {tid}\"\n                alert_queue.append({'type': 'erratic', 'id': tid, 'time': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')})\n                send_email_alert(\"Erratic Movement Alert\", msg)\n                send_push_alert(\"Erratic Movement Alert\", msg)\n                socketio.emit('alert', {'type': 'erratic', 'id': tid, 'msg': msg})\n                alert_sent_ids.add(tid)\n                performance['alerts'] += 1\n                cv2.putText(frame, \"ERRATIC\", (c[0], c[1]-20), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.7, (0,0,255), 2)\n        frame_buffer.append(frame)\n        # Performance metrics every minute\n        if frame_idx % (FPS*60) == 0:\n            elapsed = time.time() - performance['start']\n            report = f\"Frames: {performance['frames']}, Detections: {performance['detections']}, Alerts: {performance['alerts']}, FPS: {performance['frames']/elapsed:.2f}\"\n            print(report)\n            with open(\"performance_report.txt\", \"a\") as f:\n                f.write(report + \"\\n\")\n\n# ---------------- FLASK TEMPLATES ----------------\n# Create dashboard.html in the same directory:\ndashboard_html = \"\"\"\n<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html>\n<head>\n    <title>AI Surveillance Dashboard</title>\n    <script src=\"//cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/socket.io/2.3.0/socket.io.js\"></script>\n</head>\n<body>\n    <h1>Surveillance Dashboard</h1>\n    <img                         "\"\"\"\nAI Surveillance Solution: Behavior Analysis & Anomaly Detection on RTSP Video Feeds\n\nFeatures:\n- Processes live/recorded RTSP feeds\n- Analyzes behavior: detects 'your_email@gmail.com'\nMAIL_PASSWORD = 'your_email_password'\nMAIL_RECIPIENT = 'recipient_email@gmail.com'\nPUSH_ENDPOINT = 'https://your_push_service.com/notify'\n\nLOITERING_TIME = 30        # seconds\nERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESH = 0.3  # threshold for movement variance\n\nMODEL_PATH = 'yolov5s.pt'  # Downloaded at runtime if not present\n\n# ------------------- Model Download & Load -------------------\n\ndef download_yolov5_model():\n    if not os.path.exists(MODEL_PATH):\n        print(\"Downloading YOLOv5s model...\")\n        import requests\n        url = \"https://github.com/ultralytics/yolov5/releases/download/v6.0/yolov5s.pt\"\n        r = requests.get(url)\n        with open(MODEL_PATH, 'wb') as f:\n            f.write(r.content)\n\ndownload_yolov5_model()\nmodel = torch.hub.load('ultralytics/yolov5', 'custom', path=MODEL_PATH)\nmodel.conf = 0.4  # confidence threshold\n\n# ------------------- Tracking Utilities -------------------\n\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"\n    Simple centroid-based tracker for people.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_age=60):\n        self.next_id = 1\n        self.tracks = {}  # id -> {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': timestamp}\n        self.max_age = max_age\n\n    def update(self, detections):\n        now = time.time()\n        centroids = [((x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2) for x1,y1,x2,y2 in detections]\n        assigned = set()\n        # Assign detections to tracks\n        for tid, track in self.tracks.items():\n            if len(track['centroids']) > 0:\n                last_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n                dists = [np.linalg.norm(np.array(c)-np.array(last_centroid)) for c in centroids]\n                if dists and min(dists) < 50:  # pixels\n                    idx = np.argmin(dists)\n                    track['centroids'].append(centroids[idx])\n                    track['last_seen'] = now\n                    assigned.add(idx)\n        # New tracks\n        for i, c in enumerate(centroids):\n            if i not in assigned:\n                self.tracks[self.next_id] = {\n                    'centroids': deque([c], maxlen=100),\n                    'first_seen': now,\n                    'last_seen': now\n                }\n                self.next_id += 1\n        # Remove old tracks\n        to_del = [tid for tid, track in self.tracks.items() if now - track['last_seen'] > self.max_age]\n        for tid in to_del:\n            del self.tracks[tid]\n\n    def get_tracks(self):\n        return self.tracks\n\n# ------------------- Anomaly Detection -------------------\n\ndef detect_loitering(track):\n    \"\"\"\n    Loitering: Person stays within a small area for LOITERING_TIME seconds.\n    \"\"\"\n    centroids = np.array(track['centroids'])\n    if len(centroids) < 10:\n        return False\n    duration = track['last_seen'] - track['first_seen']\n    if duration < LOITERING_TIME:\n        return False\n    spread = np.max(np.linalg.norm(centroids - centroids.mean(axis=0), axis=1))\n    if spread < 60:  # pixels\n        return True\n    return False\n\ndef detect_erratic_movement(track):\n    \"\"\"\n    Erratic movement: High variance in movement direction.\n    \"\"\"\n    centroids = np.array(track['centroids'])\n    if len(centroids) < 15:\n        return False\n    diffs = np.diff(centroids, axis=0)\n    if len(diffs) < 10:\n        return False\n    directions = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n    variance = np.var(directions)\n    if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESH:\n        return True\n    return False\n\n# ------------------- Alerting -------------------\n\ndef send_email_alert(subject, body):\n    if not EMAIL_ALERTS:\n        return\n    app = Flask(__name__)\n    app.config.update(\n        MAIL_SERVER=MAIL_SERVER,\n        MAIL_PORT=MAIL_PORT,\n        MAIL_USERNAME=MAIL_USERNAME,\n        MAIL_PASSWORD=MAIL_PASSWORD,\n        MAIL_USE_TLS=True,\n        MAIL_USE_SSL=False,\n    )\n    mail = Mail(app)\n    with app.app_context():\n        msg = Message(subject, sender=MAIL_USERNAME, recipients=[MAIL_RECIPIENT])\n        msg.body = body\n        mail.send(msg)\n\ndef send_push_alert(title, message):\n    if not PUSH_ALERTS:\n        return\n    data = {'title': title, 'message': message}\n    try:\n        requests.post(PUSH_ENDPOINT, json=data)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Push notification failed: {e}\")\n\n# ------------------- Flask Web Dashboard -------------------\n\napp = Flask(__name__)\nalert_log = deque(maxlen=100)\n\nDASHBOARD_TEMPLATE = \"\"\"\n<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html>\n<head>\n    <title>AI Surveillance Dashboard</title>\n    <style>\n api_alerts():\n    return jsonify(list(alert_log))\n\n# ------------------- Main Inference Engine -------------------\n\ndef surveillance_loop():\n    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(RTSP_URL)\n    tracker = seconds\nERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD = 0.7  # normalized\nMODEL_PATH = \"yolov5s.pt\"  # Download from https://github.com/ultralytics/yolov5/releases\n\n# --------------------------\n# EMAIL ALERT FUNCTION\n# --------------------------\ndef send_email_alert(subject, body):\n    msg = MIMEText(body)\n    msg['Subject'] = subject\n    msg['From'] = SMTP_USER\n    msg['To'] = ALERT_EMAIL\n\n    try:\n        with smtplib.SMTP(SMTP_SERVER, SMTP_PORT) as server:\n            server.starttls()\n            server.login(SMTP_USER, SMTP_PASS)\n            server.sendmail(SMTP_USER, ALERT_EMAIL, msg.as_string())\n        print(f\"Alert email sent: {subject}\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Failed to send email: {e}\")\n\n# --------------------------\n# PERSON TRACKING & ANALYSIS\n# --------------------------\nclass PersonTrack:\n    def __init__(self, track_id, bbox, timestamp):\n        self.track_id = track_id\n        self.positions = [self._center(bbox)]\n        self.bboxes = [bbox]\n        self.start_time = timestamp\n        self.last_seen = timestamp\n        self.loitering_alerted = False\n        self.erratic_alerted = False\n\n    def update(self, bbox, timestamp):\n        self.positions.append(self._center(bbox))\n        self.bboxes.append(bbox)\n        self.last_seen = timestamp\n\n    def _center(self, bbox):\n        x1, y1, x2, y2 = bbox\n        return ((x1 + x2) / 2, (y1 + y2) / 2)\n\n    def loitering(self, threshold=LOITERING_TIME_THRESHOLD):\n        if len(self.positions) < 2:\n            return False\n        duration = self.last_seen - self.start_time\n        movement = np.linalg.norm(np.array(self.positions[-1]) - np.array(self.positions[0]))\n        return duration > threshold and movement < 50  # pixels\n\n    def erratic(self, threshold=ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD):\n        if len(self.positions) < 5:\n            return False\n        diffs = [np.linalg.norm(np.array(self.positions[i]) - np.array(self.positions[i-1])) for i in range(1, len(self.positions))]\n        std = np.std(diffs)\n        mean = np.mean(diffs)\n        if mean == 0:\n            return False\n        return (std / mean) > threshold\n\n# --------------------------\n# INFERENCE ENGINE\n# --------------------------\nclass SurveillanceEngine:\n    def __init__(self, rtsp_url, model_path):\n        self.rtsp_url = rtsp_url\n        self.model = torch.hub.load('ultralytics/yolov5', 'custom', path=model_path)\n        self.tracks = {}\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.metrics = {\n            'frames_processed': 0,\n            'alerts_sent': 0,\n            'loitering_events': 0,\n            'erratic_events': 0,\n            'avg_fps': 0\n        }\n        self.frame = None\n        self.alerts = []\n        self.lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    def process_stream(self):\n        cap = cv2.VideoCapture(self.rtsp_url)\n        fps_list = []\n        while True:\n            start_time = time.time()\n            ret, frame = cap.read()\n            if not ret:\n                print(\"Failed to read frame from RTSP.\")\n                break\n\n            results = self.model(frame)\n            detections = results.xyxy[0].cpu().numpy()\n            persons = [d for d in detections if int(d[5]) == 0 and d[4] > 0.4]  # class 0 = person, confidence > 0.4\n\n            # Simple tracking: assign new IDs to each detection (for demo)\n            timestamp = time.time()\n            new_tracks = {}\n            for det in persons:\n                bbox = det[:4]\n                found = False\n                for track_id, track in self.tracks.items():\n                    if self._iou(bbox, track.bboxes[-1]) > 0.3:\n                        track.update(bbox, timestamp)\n                        new_tracks[track_id] = track\n                        found = True\n                        break\n                if not found:\n                    new_tracks[self.next_id] = PersonTrack(self.next_id, bbox, timestamp)\n                    self.next_id += 1\n\n            self.tracks = new_tracks\n\n            # Analyze tracks for anomalies\n            for track_id, track in self.tracks.items():\n                if track.loitering() and not track.loitering_alerted:\n                    self._alert(\"Loitering detected\", f\"Person {track_id} loitering at {track.positions[-1]}\")\n                    track.loitering_alerted = True\n                    self.metrics['loitering_events'] += 1\n                if track.erratic() and not track.erratic_alerted:\n                    self._alert(\"Erratic movement detected\", f\"Person {track_id} erratic movement at {track.positions[-1]}\")\n                    track.erratic_alerted = True\n                    self.metrics['erratic_events'] += 1\n\n            # Draw detections\n            for track_id, track in self.tracks.items():\n                bbox = track.bboxes[-1]\n                x1, y1, x2, y2 = map(int, bbox)\n                color = (0, 255, 0)\n                cv2.rectangle(frame, (x1, y1), (x2, y2), color, 2)\n                cv2.putText(frame, f'ID {track_id}', (x1, y1-10), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.7, color, 2)\n\n            with self.lock:\n                self.frame = frame.copy()\n\n            self.metrics['frames_processed'] += 1\n            fps = 1 / (time.time() - start_time)\n            fps_list.append(fps)\n            if len(fps_list) > 100:\n                fps_list.pop(0)\n            self.metrics['avg_fps'] = np.mean(fps_list)\n\n        cap.release()\n\n    def _alert(self, title, message):\n        self.metrics['alerts_sent'] += 1\n        self.alerts.append({'title': title, 'message': message, 'time': time.strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\")})\n        send_email_alert(title, message)\n\n    def _iou(self, boxA, boxB):\n        # Intersection over Union for tracking\n        xA = max(boxA[0], boxB[0])\n        yA = max(boxA[1], boxB[1])\n        xB = min(boxA[2], boxB[2])\n        yB = min(boxA[3], boxB[3])\n        interArea = max(0, xB - xA) * max(0, yB - yA)\n        boxAArea = (boxA[2] - boxA[0]) * (boxA[3] - boxA[1])\n        boxBArea = (boxB[2] - boxB[0]) * (boxB[3] - boxB[1])\n        iou = interArea / float(boxAArea + boxBArea - interArea)\n        return iou\n\n    def get_frame(self):\n        with self.lock:\n            if self.frame is None:\n                return None\n            ret, jpeg = cv2.imencode('.jpg', self.frame)\n            return jpeg.tobytes()\n\n    def get_alerts(self):\n        with self.lock:\n            return list(self.alerts)\n\n    def get_metrics(self):\n        with self.lock:\n            return dict(self.metrics)\n\n# --------------------------\n# WEB DASHBOARD (Flask)\n# --------------------------\napp = Flask(__name__)\nengine = SurveillanceEngine(RTSP_URL, MODEL_PATH)\n\n@app.route('/')\ndef index():\n    return render_template('index.html')\n\ndef gen_frames():\n    while True:\n        frame = engine.get_frame()\n        if frame is not None:\n            yield (b'--frame\\r\\n'\n                   b'Content-Type: image/jpeg\\r\\n\\r\\n' + frame + b'\\r\\n')\n\n@app.route('/video_feed')\ndef video_feed():\n    return Response(gen_frames(), mimetype='multipart/x-mixed-replace; boundary=frame')\n\n@app.route('/alerts')\ndef alerts():\n    return jsonify(engine.get_alerts())\n\n@app.route('/metrics')\ndef metrics():\n    return jsonify(engine.get_metrics())\n\n# --------------------------\n# HTML TEMPLATE (dashboard)\n# --------------------------\nTEMPLATE = \"\"\"\n<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html>\n<head>\n    <title>AI Surveillance                         "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\nimport numpy as np\nfrom collections import deque\nimport types\nimport sys\n\n# Import functions/classes from the user code.\n# Since the code is not in a module, we will redefine the relevant classes/functions here for testing.\n\n# --- Copied from user code: SimpleTracker, detect_loitering, detect_erratic, send_email_alert, send_push_alert ---\n\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n        centroids = np.array([[(x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2] for x1, y1, x2, y2 in detections])\n        assigned = set()\n        updated_tracks = dict()\n        # Assign detections to existing tracks\n        for tid, track in self.tracks.items():\n            if len(track['centroids']) == 0:\n                continue\n            prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n            min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n            if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # Threshold\n                assigned.add(min_idx)\n                new_centroids = track['centroids']\n                new_centroids.append(centroids[min_idx])\n                updated_tracks[tid] = {'centroids': new_centroids, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        # New tracks\n        for i, c in enumerate(centroids):\n            if i not in assigned:\n                updated_tracks[self.next_id] = {'centroids': deque([c], maxlen=100), 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n                self.next_id += 1\n        # Remove lost tracks\n        self.tracks = {tid: tr for tid, tr in updated_tracks.items() if frame_idx - tr['last_seen'] < self.max_lost}\n        return self.tracks\n\n# Constants for test\nFPS = 10\nLOITERING_TIME_SEC = 30\nERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD = 0.7\n\ndef detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time):\n    \"\"\"Detects people staying in same area for LOITERING_TIME_SEC.\"\"\"\n    loitering_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        if len(tr['centroids']) < FPS * LOITERING_TIME_SEC:\n            continue\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        spread = np.linalg.norm(positions - positions.mean(axis=0), axis=1)\n        if np.max(spread) < 40:  # 40 pixels radius\n            loitering_ids.append(tid)\n    return loitering_ids\n\ndef detect_erratic(tracks):\n    \"\"\"Detects erratic movement by high variance in direction.\"\"\"\n    erratic_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        if len(positions) < 10:\n            continue\n        diffs = np.diff(positions, axis=0)\n        angles = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n        variance = np.var(angles)\n        if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD:\n            erratic_ids.append(tid)\n    return erratic_ids\n\ndef send_email_alert(subject, body):\n    #                         "import unittest\nimport numpy as np\nfrom collections import deque\n\n# Import functions/classes to test from the provided code.\n# For this test suite, we assume the following functions/classes are available:\n# - SimpleTracker\n# - detect_loitering\n# - detect_erratic\n# - send_email_alert\n# - send_push_alert\n\n# Since the original code is not modularized, we will redefine the relevant classes and functions here for testing.\n\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n        if len(detections) == 0:\n            # Remove lost tracks if no detections\n            self.tracks = {tid: tr for tid, tr in self.tracks.items() if frame_idx - tr['last_seen'] < self.max_lost}\n            return self.tracks\n\n        centroids = np.array([[(x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2] for x1, y1, x2, y2 in detections])\n        assigned = set()\n        updated_tracks = dict()\n        # Threshold\n                assigned.add(min_idx)\n                new_centroids = deque(track['centroids'], maxlen=100)\n                new_centroids.append(centroids[min_idx])\n                updated_tracks[tid] = {'centroids': new_centroids, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        # 40 pixels radius\n            loitering_ids.append(tid)\n    return loitering_ids\n\ndef detect_erratic(tracks, ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD=0.7):\n    \"\"\"Detects erratic movement by high variance in direction.\"\"\"\n    erratic_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        if len(positions) < 10:\n            continue\n        diffs = np.diff(positions, axis=0)\n        angles = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n        variance = np.var(angles)\n        if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD:\n            erratic_ids.append(tid)\n    return erratic_ids\n\n# Mocks for alerting (no actual email/push sent)\ndef send_email_alert(subject, body):\n    send_email_alert.last_call = (subject, body)\n    return True\nsend_email_alert.last_call = None\n\ndef send_push_alert(title, message):\n    send_push_alert.last_call = (title, message)\n    return True\nsend_push_alert.last_call = None\n\nclass TestSimpleTracker(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.tracker = SimpleTracker(max_lost=2)\n\n    def test_single_detection(self):\n        #                         "import unittest\nimport numpy as np\nfrom collections import deque\nimport sys\n\n# Import functions/classes to test from the original code\n# For this test suite, we assume the following classes/functions are available:\n# - SimpleTracker\n# - detect_loitering\n# - detect_erratic\n# - send_email_alert\n# - send_push_alert\n\n# If the code is in surveillance.py, you could do:\n# from surveillance import SimpleTracker, detect_loitering, detect_erratic\n\n# For this test, we'll redefine minimal versions of the relevant classes/functions\n# to allow the test suite to run independently of the heavy dependencies and side effects.\n\n# --- Minimal implementations for testability ---\n\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n        centroids = np.array([[(x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2] for x1, y1, x2, y2 in detections])\n        assigned = set()\n        updated_tracks = dict()\n        # Assign detections to existing tracks\n        for tid, track in self.tracks.items():\n            if len(track['centroids']) == 0:\n                continue\n            prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n            min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n            if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # Threshold\n                assigned.add(min_idx)\n                new_centroids = track['centroids']\n                new_centroids.append(centroids[min_idx])\n                updated_tracks[tid] = {'centroids': new_centroids, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        # New tracks\n        for i, c in enumerate(centroids):\n            if i not in assigned:\n                updated_tracks[self.next_id] = {'centroids': deque([c], maxlen=100), 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n                self.next_id += 1\n        # Simulate a person moving slightly\n        tracks = self.tracker.update([(10, 10, 20, 20)], frame_idx=1)\n        tid = list(tracks.keys())[0]\n        tracks = self.tracker.update([(12, 12, 22, 22)], frame_idx=2)\n        self.assertIn(tid, tracks)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks[tid]['centroids']), 2)\n        # Add track, then skip frames to remove it\n        self.tracker.update([(10, 10, 20, 20)], frame_idx=1)\n        for i in range(2, 10):\n            self.tracker.update([], frame_idx=i)\n        self.assertEqual(len(self.tracker.tracks), 0)\n\nclass TestDetectLoitering(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_no_loitering_when_not_enough_points(self):\n        tracks = {0: {'centroids': deque([[10, 10]]*5, maxlen=100)}}\n        result = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time=1, FPS=10, LOITERING_TIME_SEC=10)\n        self.assertEqual(result, [])\n\n    def test_loitering_detected_with_low_spread(self):\n        # Simulate 100 points spread out\n        points = np.linspace([0,0], [500,500], 100).astype(int)\n        tracks = {0: {'centroids': deque(points, maxlen=100)}}\n        result = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time=100/10, FPS=10, LOITERING_TIME_SEC=10)\n        self.assertNotIn(0, result)\n\nclass TestDetectErratic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_no_erratic_with_straight_line(self):\n        #                     "best_tests": "import unittest\nimport numpy as np\nfrom collections import deque\n\n# Import functions/classes to test from the provided code.\n# We'll assume the following classes and functions are available in the same namespace:\n# - SimpleTracker\n# - detect_loitering\n# - detect_erratic\n\n# We'll redefine minimal versions here for testing purposes, since the code is not in a module.\n\n# --- Begin: Minimal code extraction for testing ---\n\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n        if len(detections) == 0:\n            # Remove tracks that are too old\n            self.tracks = {tid: tr for tid, tr in self.tracks.items() if frame_idx - tr['last_seen'] < self.max_lost}\n            return self.tracks\n        centroids = np.array([[(x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2] for x1, y1, x2, y2 in detections])\n        assigned = set()\n        updated_tracks = dict()\n        # Assign detections to existing tracks\n        for tid, track in self.tracks.items():\n            if len(track['centroids']) == 0:\n                continue\n            prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n            min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n            if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # Threshold\n                assigned.add(min_idx)\n                new_centroids = track['centroids'].copy()\n                new_centroids.append(centroids[min_idx])\n                updated_tracks[tid] = {'centroids': new_centroids, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        # New tracks\n        for i, c in enumerate(centroids):\n            if i not in assigned:\n                updated_tracks[self.next_id] = {'centroids': deque([c], maxlen=100), 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n                self.next_id += 1\n        # Remove lost tracks\n        self.tracks = {tid: tr for tid, tr in updated_tracks.items() if frame_idx - tr['last_seen'] < self.max_lost}\n        return self.tracks\n\ndef detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time, FPS=10, LOITERING_TIME_SEC=30):\n    \"\"\"Detects people staying in same area for LOITERING_TIME_SEC.\"\"\"\n    loitering_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        if len(tr['centroids']) < FPS * LOITERING_TIME_SEC:\n            continue\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        spread = np.linalg.norm(positions - positions.mean(axis=0), axis=1)\n        if np.max(spread) < 40:  # 40 pixels radius\n            loitering_ids.append(tid)\n    return loitering_ids\n\ndef detect_erratic(tracks, ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD=0.7):\n    \"\"\"Detects erratic movement by high variance in direction.\"\"\"\n    erratic_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        if len(positions) < 10:\n            continue\n        diffs = np.diff(positions, axis=0)\n        angles = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n        variance = np.var(angles)\n        if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD:\n            erratic_ids.append(tid)\n    return erratic_ids\n\n# --- End: Minimal code extraction for testing ---\n\nclass TestSimpleTracker(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.tracker = SimpleTracker(max_lost=5)\n\n    def test_single_detection(self):\n        # One detection, should create one track\n        dets = [(10, 10, 20, 20)]\n        tracks = self.tracker.update(dets, 0)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 1)\n        tid = list(tracks.keys())[0]\n        centroid = tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1]\n        self.assertTrue(np.allclose(centroid, [15, 15]))\n\n    def test_multiple_detections(self):\n        dets = [(10, 10, 20, 20), (100, 100, 110, 110)]\n        tracks = self.tracker.update(dets, 0)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 2)\n        centroids = [tr['centroids'][-1] for tr in tracks.values()]\n        self.assertIn([15, 15], centroids)\n        self.assertIn([105, 105], centroids)\n\n    def test_track_assignment(self):\n        # Simulate a moving object\n        dets1 = [(10, 10, 20, 20)]\n        dets2 = [(12, 12, 22, 22)]  # Should be assigned to same track\n        self.tracker.update(dets1, 0)\n        tracks = self.tracker.update(dets2, 1)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 1)\n        tid = list(tracks.keys())[0]\n        centroids = list(tracks[tid]['centroids'])\n        self.assertTrue(np.allclose(centroids[0], [15, 15]))\n        self.assertTrue(np.allclose(centroids[1], [17, 17]))\n\n    def test_track_removal(self):\n        # No detections for max_lost frames, track should be removed\n        dets = [(10, 10, 20, 20)]\n        self.tracker.update(dets, 0)\n        for i in range(1, 7):\n            self.tracker.update([], i)\n        self.assertEqual(len(self.tracker.tracks), 0)\n\n    def test_track_persistence(self):\n        # Track should persist if lost less than max_lost frames\n        dets = [(10, 10, 20, 20)]\n        self.tracker.update(dets, 0)\n        for i in range(1, 5):\n            self.tracker.update([], i)\n        self.assertEqual(len(self.tracker.tracks), 1)\n\nclass TestDetectLoitering(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_loitering_detected(self):\n        # Simulate a track with centroids in a small area for enough frames\n        tid = 1\n        centroids = deque([[100, 100]] * 300, maxlen=1000)  # 30s at FPS=10\n        tracks = {tid: {'centroids': centroids}}\n        result = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time=30, FPS=10, LOITERING_TIME_SEC=30)\n        self.assertIn(tid, result)\n\n    def test_loitering_not_detected_short_time(self):\n        # Not enough frames\n        tid = 1\n        centroids = deque([[100, 100]] * 50, maxlen=1000)\n        tracks = {tid: {'centroids': centroids}}\n        result = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time=5, FPS=10, LOITERING_TIME_SEC=30)\n        self.assertNotIn(tid, result)\n\n    def test_loitering_not_detected_large_spread(self):\n        # Centroids spread out\n        tid = 1\n        centroids = deque([[100+i, 100] for i in range(300)], maxlen=1000)\n        tracks = {tid: {'centroids': centroids}}\n        result = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time=30, FPS=10, LOITERING_TIME_SEC=30)\n        self.assertNotIn(tid, result)\n\n    def test_multiple_tracks(self):\n        tracks = {\n            1: {'centroids': deque([[100, 100]] * 300, maxlen=1000)},\n            2: {'centroids': deque([[200+i, 200] for i in range(300)], maxlen=1000)}\n        }\n        result = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time=30, FPS=10, LOITERING_TIME_SEC=30)\n        self.assertIn(1, result)\n        self.assertNotIn(2, result)\n\nclass TestDetectErratic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_erratic_detected(self):\n        # Simulate a track with high variance in direction\n        tid = 1\n        # Move in a circle\n        centroids = deque([[100 + int(20*np.cos(t)), 100 + int(20*np.sin(t))] for t in np.linspace(0, 6.28, 30)], maxlen=1000)\n        tracks = {tid: {'centroids': centroids}}\n        result = detect_erratic(tracks, ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD=0.5)\n        self.assertIn(tid, result)\n\n    def test_erratic_not_detected_straight_line(self):\n        tid = 1\n        centroids = deque([[100 + i, 100] for i in range(30)], maxlen=1000)\n        tracks = {tid: {'centroids': centroids}}\n        result = detect_erratic(tracks, ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD=0.5)\n        self.assertNotIn(tid, result)\n\n    def test_erratic_not_detected_short_track(self):\n        tid = 1\n        centroids = deque([[100 + i, 100] for i in range(5)], maxlen=1000)\n        tracks = {tid: {'centroids': centroids}}\n        result = detect_erratic(tracks, ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD=0.5)\n        self.assertNotIn(tid, result)\n\n    def test_multiple_tracks(self):\n        tracks = {\n            1: {'centroids': deque([[100 + int(20*np.cos(t)), 100 + int(20*np.sin(t))] for t in np.linspace(0, 6.28, 30)], maxlen=1000)},\n            2: {'centroids': deque([[200 + i, 200] for i in range(30)], maxlen=1000)}\n        }\n        result = detect_erratic(tracks, ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD=0.5)\n        self.assertIn(1, result)\n        self.assertNotIn(2, result)\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",

  msg.set_content(body)\n    try:\n        with smtplib.SMTP(SMTP_SERVER, SMTP_PORT) as server:\n            server.starttls()\n            server.login(EMAIL_SENDER, EMAIL_PASSWORD)\n (b'--frame\\r\\n'\n                   b'Content-Type: image/jpeg\\r\\n\\r\\n' + frame_bytes + b'\\r\\n')\n        time.sleep(1/FPS)\n\n@app.route('/video_feed')\ndef video_feed():\n    return cv2.VideoCapture(RTSP_URL)\n    tracker = SimpleTracker()\n    frame_idx = 0\n    alert_sent_ids = set()\n    performance = {'frames': 0, 'detections': 0, 'alerts': 0, 'start': time.time()}\n    # Get the camera FPS (fallback to 25 if not available)\n    cam_fps = cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FPS)\n    if cam_fps <= 0 or cam_fps > 120:\n        cam_fps = 25\n    frame_skip = max(1, int(cam_fps // FPS))\n != 0:\n            continue  # Downsample FPS\n        results = model(frame)\n        detections = []\n        for *xyxy, conf, cls in results.xyxy[0].cpu().numpy():\n            if int(cls) == 0:  # person class in COCO\n                x1, y1, x2, y2 = map(int, xyxy)\n                detections.append((x1, y1, x2, y2))\n                cv2.rectangle(frame, (x1, y1), (x2, y2), (0,255,0), 2)\n        performance['frames'] += 1\n        performance['detections'] += len(detections)\n        tracks = tracker.update(detections, frame_idx)\n        # Draw tracks\n        for tid, tr in loitering_ids = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_idx/FPS)\n        erratic_ids = detect_erratic(tracks)\n        for tid in loitering_ids:\n            if tid not in alert_sent_ids:\n                c = %H:%M:%S')})\n                send_email_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                send_push_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                socketio.emit('alert', {'type': 'loitering', 'id': tid, 'msg': msg})\n                alert_sent_ids.add(tid)\n                performance['alerts'] += 1\n                cv2.putText(frame, \"LOITERING\", (c[0], c[1]-20), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.7, (0,0,255), 2)\n        for tid in erratic_ids:\n            if tid not in alert_sent_ids:\n                c = tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1]\n                msg = f\"Erratic movement detected for ID {tid}\"\n                alert_queue.append({'type': 'erratic', 'id': tid, 'time': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')})\n                send_email_alert(\"Erratic Movement Alert\", msg)\n                send_push_alert(\"Erratic Movement Alert\", msg)\n                socketio.emit('alert', {'type': 'erratic', 'id': tid, 'msg': msg})\n                alert_sent_ids.add(tid)\n metrics every minute\n        if frame_idx % (FPS*60) == 0:\n            elapsed = time.time() - performance['start']\n            report = f\"Frames: {performance['frames']}, Detections:         continue\n            prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1) if len(centroids) > 0 else np.array([])\n            if len(distances) == 0:\n                continue\n            min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n            if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # Threshold\n                assigned.add(min_idx)\n                new_centroids = track['centroids']\n                new_centroids.append(centroids[min_idx])\n                updated_tracks[tid] = {'centroids': new_centroids, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        # New tracks\n        for i, c in enumerate(centroids):\n            if i not in assigned:\n                updated_tracks[self.next_id] = {'centroids': deque([c], maxlen=100), 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n                self.next_id += 1\n        # Remove lost tracks\n        self.tracks = {tid: tr for tid, tr in updated_tracks.items() if frame_idx - tr['last_seen'] < self.max_lost}\n        return self.tracks\n\n# ---------------- ANOMALY DETECTION ----------------\ndef detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time):\n    \"\"\"Detects people staying in same area for LOITERING_TIME_SEC.\"\"\"\n    loitering_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        if len(tr['centroids']) < FPS * LOITERING_TIME_SEC:\n            continue\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        spread = np.linalg.norm(positions - positions.mean(axis=0), axis=1)\n        if np.max(spread) < 40:  # 40 pixels radius\n            loitering_ids.append(tid)\n    return loitering_ids\n\ndef detect_erratic(tracks):\n    \"\"\"Detects erratic movement by high variance in direction.\"\"\"\n    erratic_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        if len(positions) < 10:\n            continue\n        diffs = np.diff(positions, axis=0)\n        angles = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n        variance = np.var(angles)\n        if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD:\n            erratic_ids.append(tid)\n    return erratic_ids\n\n# ---------------- ALERTING ----------------\ndef send_email_alert(subject, body):\n    msg = EmailMessage()\n    msg['Subject'] = subject\n    msg['From'] = EMAIL_SENDER\n    msg['To'] = ALERT_EMAIL\n    msg.set_content(body)\n    try:\n        with smtplib.SMTP(SMTP_SERVER, SMTP_PORT) as server:\n            server.starttls()\n            server.login(EMAIL_SENDER, EMAIL_PASSWORD)\n            server.send_message(msg)\n        print(f\"Email alert sent: {subject}\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Email alert failed: {e}\")\n\ndef send_push_alert(title, message):\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(PUSH_API_URL, json={'title': title, 'message': message})\n        print(f\"Push alert sent: {resp.status_code}\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Push alert failed: {e}\")\n\n# ---------------- WEB DASHBOARD ----------------\napp = Flask(__name__, template_folder=\"templates\")\nsocketio = SocketIO(app)\n\nalert_queue = deque(maxlen=10)\nframe_buffer = deque(maxlen=1)\n\n@app.route('/')\ndef index():\n    return render_template('dashboard.html')\n\n@app.route('/alerts')\ndef get_alerts():\n    return jsonify(list(alert_queue))\n\ndef gen_frames():\n    while True:\n        if        b'Content-Type: image/jpeg\\r\\n\\r\\n' + frame_bytes + b'\\r\\n')\n        time.sleep(1/FPS)\n\n@app.route('/video_feed')\ndef video_feed():\n    return Response(gen_frames(), mimetype='multipart/x-mixed-replace; boundary=frame')\n\n# ---------------- MAIN INFERENCE LOOP ----------------\ndef surveillance_loop():\n    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(RTSP_URL)\n    tracker = SimpleTracker()\n    frame_idx = 0\n    alert_sent_ids = set()\n    performance = {'frames': 0, 'detections': 0, 'alerts': 0, 'start': time.time()}\n    last_fps_check = time.time()\n    while True:\n        ret, frame = cap.read()\n        if not ret or frame is None:\n            print(\"Failed to read frame. Reconnecting...\")\n            cap.release()\n            time.sleep(2)\n            cap = cv2.VideoCapture(RTSP_URL)\n            continue\n        frame_idx += 1\n        # Downsample FPS\n    detections = []\n        for *xyxy, conf, cls in results.xyxy[0].cpu().numpy():\n            if int(cls) == 0:  # person class in COCO\n                x1, y1, x2, y2 = map(int, xyxy)\n                detections.append((x1, y1, x2, y2))\n                cv2.rectangle(frame, (x1, y1), (x2, y2), (0,255,0), 2)\n        performance['frames'] += 1\n        performance['detections'] += alert_queue.append({'type': 'loitering', 'id': tid, 'time': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')})\n                send_email_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                send_push_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                socketio.emit('alert', {'type': 'loitering', 'id': tid, 'msg': msg})\n                alert_sent_ids.add(tid)\n                performance['alerts'] += 1\n                c = tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1]\n                cv2.putText(frame, \"LOITERING\", (c[0], c[1]-20), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.7, (0,0,255), 2)\n                         "import unittest\nfrom collections import deque\nimport numpy as np\nimport types\n\n# Import relevant classes and functions from the code under test\n# We'll redefine the relevant classes and functions here for testing, since the original code is not in a module.\n\n# --- SimpleTracker (copied from code) ---\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n        centroids = np.array([[(x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2] for x1, y1, x2, y2 in detections])\n        assigned = set()\n        updated_tracks = dict()\n        # Assign detections to existing tracks\n        for tid, track in self.tracks.items():\n            if len(track['centroids']) == 0:\n                continue\n            prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            if len(centroids) > 0:\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n                min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n                if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # Threshold\n                    assigned.add(min_idx)\n                    new_centroids = track['centroids'].copy()\n                    new_centroids.append(centroids[min_idx])\n                    updated_tracks[tid] = {'centroids': new_centroids, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        # New tracks\n        for i, c in enumerate(centroids):\n            if i not in assigned:\n                updated_tracks[self.next_id] = {'centroids': deque([c], maxlen=100), 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n                self.next_id += 1\n        # Remove lost tracks\n        self.tracks = {tid: tr for tid, tr in updated_tracks.items() if frame_idx - tr['last_seen'] < self.max_lost}\n        return self.tracks\n\n# --- Anomaly Detection Functions (copied from code) ---\nFPS = 10\nLOITERING_TIME_SEC = 30\nERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD = 0.7\n\ndef detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time):\n    \"\"\"Detects people staying in same area for LOITERING_TIME_SEC.\"\"\"\n    loitering_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        if len(tr['centroids']) < FPS * LOITERING_TIME_SEC:\n            continue\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        spread = np.linalg.norm(positions - positions.mean(axis=0), axis=1)\n        if np.max(spread) < 40:  # 40 pixels radius\n            loitering_ids.append(tid)\n    return loitering_ids\n\ndef detect_erratic(tracks):\n    \"\"\"Detects erratic movement by high variance in direction.\"\"\"\n    erratic_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        if len(positions) < 10:\n            continue\n        diffs = np.diff(positions, axis=0)\n        angles = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n        variance = np.var(angles)\n        if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD:\n            erratic_ids.append(tid)\n    return erratic_ids\n\n# --- Alerting (mocked for test) ---\ndef send_email_alert(subject, body):\n    send_email_alert.called = True\n    send_email_alert.last_subject = subject\n    send_email_alert.last_body = body\n\ndef send_push_alert(title, message):\n    send_push_alert.called = True\n    send_push_alert.last_title = title\n    send_push_alert.last_message = message\n\n# --- Test Suite ---\nclass TestSimpleTracker(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.tracker = SimpleTracker(max_lost=5)\n\n    def test_single_detection_new_track(self):\n        tracks = self.tracker.update([(10, 10, 30, 30)], 1)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 1)\n        tid = list(tracks.keys())[0]\n        centroid = tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1]\n        self.assertTrue(np.allclose(centroid, [20, 20]))\n\n    def test_multiple_detections_new_tracks(self):\n        dets = [(10, 10, 30, 30), (100, 100, 120, 120)]\n        tracks = self.tracker.update(dets, 1)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 2)\n        centroids = [tr['centroids'][-1] for tr in tracks.values()]\n        self.assertTrue(any(np.allclose(c, [20, 20]) for c in centroids))\n        self.assertTrue(any(np.allclose(c, [110, 110]) for c in centroids))\n\n    def test_track_assignment(self):\n        #                         "import unittest\nfrom collections import deque\nimport numpy as np\nimport types\n\n# Mock configuration values for testing\nFPS = 10\nLOITERING_TIME_SEC = 30\nERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD = 0.7\n\n# --- Copy the relevant code from the original for isolated testing ---\n\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n        centroids = np.array([[(x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2] for x1, y1, x2, y2 in detections])\n        assigned = set()\n        updated_tracks = dict()\n        # Assign detections to existing tracks\n        for tid, track in self.tracks.items():\n            if len(track['centroids']) == 0:\n                continue\n            prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            if len(centroids) > 0:\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n                min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n                if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # Threshold\n                    assigned.add(min_idx)\n                    new_centroids = track['centroids'].copy()\n                    new_centroids.append(centroids[min_idx])\n                    updated_tracks[tid] = {'centroids': new_centroids, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        # New tracks\n        for i, c in enumerate(centroids):\n            if i not in assigned:\n                updated_tracks[self.next_id] = {'centroids': deque([c], maxlen=100), 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n                self.next_id += 1\n        # Remove lost tracks\n        self.tracks = {tid: tr for tid, tr in updated_tracks.items() if frame_idx - tr['last_seen'] < self.max_lost}\n        return self.tracks\n\ndef detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time):\n    \"\"\"Detects people staying in same area for LOITERING_TIME_SEC.\"\"\"\n    loitering_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        if len(tr['centroids']) < FPS * LOITERING_TIME_SEC:\n            continue\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        spread = np.linalg.norm(positions - positions.mean(axis=0), axis=1)\n        if np.max(spread) < 40:  # 40 pixels radius\n            loitering_ids.append(tid)\n    return loitering_ids\n\ndef detect_erratic(tracks):\n    \"\"\"Detects erratic movement by high variance in direction.\"\"\"\n    erratic_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        if len(positions) < 10:\n            continue\n        diffs = np.diff(positions, axis=0)\n        angles = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n        variance = np.var(angles)\n        if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD:\n            erratic_ids.append(tid)\n    return erratic_ids\n\n# --- Begin Test Suite ---\n\nclass TestSimpleTracker(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.tracker = SimpleTracker(max_lost=5)\n\n    def test_single_detection_creates_track(self):\n        tracks = self.tracker.update([(0, 0, 10, 10)], 1)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 1)\n        tid = list(tracks.keys())[0]\n        self.assertEqual(tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1][0], 5)\n        self.assertEqual(tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1][1], 5)\n\n    def test_multiple_detections_create_multiple_tracks(self):\n        tracks = self.tracker.update([(0, 0, 10, 10), (100, 100, 110, 110)], 1)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 2)\n        centroids = [tr['centroids'][-1] for tr in tracks.values()]\n        self.assertTrue(any(np.allclose(c, [5,5]) for c in centroids))\n        self.assertTrue(any(np.allclose(c, [105,105]) for c in centroids))\n\n    def test_track_assignment(self):\n        # Add a track, lose it, then new detection\n        self.tracker.update([(0, 0, 10, 10)], 1)\n        for i in range(2, 8):\n            self.tracker.update([], i)\n        tracks = self.tracker.update([(20, 20, 30, 30)], 8)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 1)\n        # Should have new track id (not 0)\n        self.assertNotIn(0, tracks)\n\n    def test_multiple_tracks_and_assignment(self):\n        # Add two tracks\n        self.tracker.update([(0, 0, 10, 10), (100, 100, 110, 110)], 1)\n        #                         "import unittest\nfrom collections import deque\nimport numpy as np\n\n# --- Mocks for testing (since original code depends on hardware, network, and Flask) ---\n\n# Mock SimpleTracker (copied from the provided code)\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n        centroids = np.array([[(x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2] for x1, y1, x2, y2 in detections])\n        assigned = set()\n        updated_tracks = dict()\n        # Assign detections to existing tracks\n        for tid, track in self.tracks.items():\n            if len(track['centroids']) == 0:\n                continue\n            prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            if len(centroids) > 0:\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n                min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n                if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # 40 pixels radius\n            loitering_ids.append(tid)\n    return loitering_ids\n\ndef detect_erratic(tracks):\n    \"\"\"Detects erratic movement by high variance in direction.\"\"\"\n    erratic_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        if len(positions) < 10:\n            continue\n        diffs = np.diff(positions, axis=0)\n        angles = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n        variance = np.var(angles)\n        if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD:\n            erratic_ids.append(tid)\n    return erratic_ids\n\n# --- TEST SUITE ---\n\nclass TestSimpleTracker(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.tracker = SimpleTracker()\n        self.frame_idx = 0\n\n    def test_no_detections(self):\n        tracks = self.tracker.update([], self.frame_idx)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 0)\n\n    def test_single_detection(self):\n        det = [(10, 10, 30, 30)]\n        tracks = self.tracker.update(det, self.frame_idx)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 1)\n        tid = list(tracks.keys())[0]\n        centroid = tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1]\n        self.assertTrue(np.allclose(centroid, [20, 20]))\n\n    def test_multiple_detections(self):\n        dets = [(10, 10, 30, 30), (100, 100, 120, 120)]\n        tracks = self.tracker.update(dets, self.frame_idx)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 2)\n        centroids = [tr['centroids'][-1] for tr in tracks.values()]\n        self.assertTrue(any(np.allclose(c, [20, 20]) for c in centroids))\n        self.assertTrue(any(np.allclose(c, [110, 110]) for c in centroids))\n\n    def test_track_assignment(self):\n        # Simulate missing detection for >max_lost frames\n        for i in range(self.tracker.max_lost + 1):\n            self.frame_idx += 1\n            tracks = self.tracker.update([], self.frame_idx)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tracks), 0)\n\nclass TestAnomalyDetection(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Enough frames, little movement\n        tr = {'centroids': deque([[100,100] for _ in range(FPS*LOITERING_TIME_SEC)], maxlen=100)}\n        tracks = {self.tid: tr}\n        ids = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time=LOITERING_TIME_SEC)\n        self.assertIn(self.tid, ids)\n\n    def test_no_loitering_if_moving(self):\n        # Enough frames, but person moves a lot\n        tr = {'centroids': deque([[i*10, i*10] for i in range(FPS*LOITERING_TIME_SEC)], maxlen=100)}\n        tracks = {self.tid: tr}\n        ids = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time=LOITERING_TIME_SEC)\n        self.assertNotIn(self.tid, ids)\n\n    def test_no_erratic_short_track(self):\n        tr = {'centroids': deque([[i, i] for i in range(9)], maxlen=100)}\n        tracks = {self.tid: tr}\n        ids = detect_erratic(tracks)\n        self.assertEqual(ids, [])\n\n    def test_erratic_detected(self):\n        # the camera FPS (fallback to 25 if not available)\n    cam_fps = cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FPS)\n    if cam_fps <= 0 or cam_fps > 120:\n        cam_fps = 25\n    frame_skip = max(1, int(cam_fps // FPS))\n    while True:\n        ret, frame = cap.read()\n        if not ret:\n            print(\"Failed to read frame. Reconnecting...\")\n            cap.release()\n            time.sleep(2)\n            cap = cv2.VideoCapture(RTSP_URL)\n            continue\n        frame_idx += 1\n        if frame_idx % frame_skip != 0:\n            continue  # Downsample FPS\n        results = model(frame)\n        detections = []\n        for *xyxy, conf, cls in results.xyxy[0].cpu().numpy():\n            if int(cls) == 0:  # person class in COCO\n                x1, y1, x2, y2 = map(int, xyxy)\n                detections.append((x1, y1, x2, y2))\n                cv2.rectangle(frame, (x1, y1), (x2, y2), (0,255,0), 2)\n        performance['frames'] += 1\n        performance['detections'] += len(detections)\n        tracks = tracker.update(detections, frame_idx)\n        # Draw tracks\n        for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n            c = tr['centroids'][-1]\n            cv2.putText(frame, f\"ID:{tid}\", (c[0], c[1]), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.5, (255,0,0), 2)\n        # Anomaly detection\n        loitering_ids = detect_loitering(tracks, frame_idx/FPS)\n        erratic_ids = detect_erratic(tracks)\n        for tid in loitering_ids:\n            if tid not in alert_sent_ids:\n                c = tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1]\n                msg = f\"Loitering detected for ID {tid}\"\n                alert_queue.append({'type': 'loitering', 'id': tid, 'time': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')})\n                send_email_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                send_push_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                socketio.emit('alert', {'type': 'loitering', 'id': tid, 'msg': msg})\n                alert_sent_ids.add(tid)\n                performance['alerts'] += 1\n                cv2.putText(frame, \"LOITERING\", (c[0], c[1]-20), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.7, (0,0,255), 2)\n        for tid in erratic_ids:\n            if tid not in alert_sent_ids:\n                c = tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1]\n                msg = f\"Erratic movement detected for ID {tid}\"\n                alert_queue.append({'type': 'erratic', 'id': tid, 'time': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')})\n                send_email_alert(\"Erratic Movement Alert\", msg)\n                send_push_alert(\"Erratic Movement Alert\", msg)\n                socketio.emit('alert', {'type': 'erratic', 'id': tid, 'msg': msg})\n                alert_sent_ids.add(tid)\n                performance['alerts'] += 1\n                cv2.putText(frame, \"ERRATIC\", (c[0], c[1]-20), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.7, (0,0,255), 2)\n        frame_buffer.append(frame)\n        # Performance metrics every minute\n        if frame_idx % (FPS*60) == 0:\n            elapsed = time.time() - performance['start']\n            report = f\"Frames: {performance['frames']}, Detections: {performance['detections']}, Alerts: {performance['alerts']}, FPS: {performance['frames']/elapsed:.2f}\"\n            print(report)\n            with open(\"performance_report.txt\", \"a\") as f:\n                f.write(report + \"\\n\")\n\n# ---------------- FLASK TEMPLATES ----------------\n# Create dashboard.html in the templates directory if not exists\nos.makedirs(\"templates\", exist_ok=True)\ndashboard_html = \"\"\"\n<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html>\n<head>\n    <title>AI Surveillance Dashboard</title>\n    <script src=\"//cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/socket.io/2.3.0/socket.io.js\"></script>\n</head>\n<body>\n    <h1>Surveillance Dashboard</h1>\n    <img src=\"/video_feed\" width=\"720\">\n    <h2>Alerts</h2>\n    <ul id=\"alerts\"></ul>\n    <script>\n        var socket = io();\n        socket.on('alert', function(data) {\n            var alerts = document.getElementById('alerts');\n            var li = document.createElement('li');\n            li.innerText = data.type + \" for ID \" + data.id + \": \" + data.msg;\n            alerts.appendChild(li);\n        });\n        function refreshAlerts() {\n            fetch('/alerts').then(resp => resp.json()).then(data => {\n                var alerts = document.getElementById('alerts');\n                alerts.innerHTML = '';\n                data.forEach(function(a) {\n                    var li = document.createElement('li');\n                    li.innerText = a.type + \" for ID \" + a.id + \" at \" + a.time;\n                    alerts.appendChild(li);\n                });\n            });\n        }\n        setInterval(refreshAlerts, 5000);\n    </script>\n</body>\n</html>\n\"\"\"\nwith open(\"templates/dashboard.html\", \"w\") as f:\n    f.write(dashboard_html)\n\n# ---------------- DOCKERFILE ----------------\ndockerfile_content = \"\"\"\n# Dockerfile for AI Surveillance Solution\nFROM python:3.8-slim\nWORKDIR /app\nCOPY . /app\nRUN pip install torch torchvision opencv-python flask flask-socketio tqdm requests\nEXPOSE 5000\nCMD [\"python\", \"surveillance.py\"]\n\"\"\"\nwith open(\"Dockerfile\", \"w\") as                         "\"\"\"\nAI Surveillance Solution: Behavior Analysis & Anomaly Detection from RTSP Video Feeds\n\nFeatures:\n- Processes live or recorded RTSP streams\n- Detects loitering and erratic movement (anomaly detection)\n- Sends alerts via web dashboard (Flask), email, and push notifications\n- Includes model files, Docker deployment, and performance metrics report\n\nDependencies:\n- Python 3.8+\n- PyTorch\n- OpenCV\n- Flask\n- Flask-SocketIO\n- smtplib (built-in)\n- requests (for push notifications)\n- numpy\n- tqdm\n\nInstructions:\n- Place this script in a directory.\n- Download the pre-trained YOLOv5 model weights (`yolov5s.pt`) from https://github.com/ultralytics/yolov5/releases\n- Adjust RTSP_URL, email settings, and PUSH_API_URL as needed.\n- To run: `python surveillance.py`\n- To build Docker image: see provided Dockerfile below.\n\nNote: This is a simplified prototype for demonstration purposes.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport cv2\nimport torch\nimport numpy as np\nimport time\nimport threading\nfrom collections import deque\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template, Response, jsonify\nfrom flask_socketio import SocketIO, emit\nimport smtplib\nfrom email.message import EmailMessage\nimport requests\nfrom tqdm import tqdm\n\n# ---------------- CONFIGURATION ----------------\nRTSP_URL = \"rtsp://username:password@camera_ip:554/stream\"  # <-- Set your RTSP URL here\nMODEL_PATH = \"yolov5s.pt\"  # Download from Ultralytics\nALERT_EMAIL = \"alert_receiver@example.com\"\nEMAIL_SENDER = \"your_email@example.com\"\nEMAIL_PASSWORD = \"your_email_password\"\nSMTP_SERVER = \"smtp.gmail.com\"\nSMTP_PORT = 587\nPUSH_API_URL = \"https://your_push_service.com/api/notify\"\nLOITERING_TIME_SEC = 30  # Time threshold for loitering (seconds)\nERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD = 0.7  # Movement variance threshold\nFPS = 10  # Frames per second to process\n\n# ---------------- MODEL LOADING ----------------\nprint(\"Loading YOLOv5 model...\")\nmodel = torch.hub.load('ultralytics/yolov5', 'custom', path=MODEL_PATH)\nmodel.conf = 0.4  # Confidence threshold\n\n# ---------------- TRACKING UTILS ----------------\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n        centroids = np.array([[(x1+x2)//2, (y1+y2)//2] for x1, y1, x2, y2 in detections])\n        assigned = set()\n        updated_tracks = dict()\n        # Assign detections to existing tracks\n        for tid, track in self.tracks.items():\n            if len(track['centroids']) == 0:\n                continue\n            prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            if len(centroids) > 0:\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n                min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n                if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # Threshold\n                    assigned.add(min_idx)\n                    new_centroids = track['centroids'].copy()\n                    new_centroids.append(centroids[min_idx])\n                    updated_tracks[tid] = {'centroids': new_centroids, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        # New tracks\n        for i, c in enumerate(centroids):\n            if i not in assigned:\n                updated_tracks[self.next_id] = {'centroids': deque([c], maxlen=100), 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n                self.next_id += 1\n        # Remove lost tracks\n        self.tracks = {tid: tr for tid, tr in updated_tracks.items() if frame_idx - tr['last_seen'] < self.max_lost}\n        return self.tracks\n\n# ---------------- ANOMALY DETECTION ----------------\ndef detect_loitering(tracks, frame_time):\n    \"\"\"Detects people staying in same area for LOITERING_TIME_SEC.\"\"\"\n    loitering_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        if len(tr['centroids']) < FPS * LOITERING_TIME_SEC:\n            continue\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        spread = np.linalg.norm(positions - positions.mean(axis=0), axis=1)\n        if np.max(spread) < 40:  # 40 pixels radius\n            loitering_ids.append(tid)\n    return loitering_ids\n\ndef detect_erratic(tracks):\n    \"\"\"Detects erratic movement by high variance in direction.\"\"\"\n    erratic_ids = []\n    for tid, tr in tracks.items():\n        positions = np.array(tr['centroids'])\n        if len(positions) < 10:\n            continue\n        diffs = np.diff(positions, axis=0)\n        angles = np.arctan2(diffs[:,1], diffs[:,0])\n        variance = np.var(angles)\n        if variance > ERRATIC_MOVEMENT_THRESHOLD:\n            erratic_ids.append(tid)\n    return erratic_ids\n\n# ---------------- ALERTING ----------------\ndef send_email_alert(subject, body):\n    msg = EmailMessage()\n    msg['Subject'] = subject\n    msg['From'] = EMAIL_SENDER\n    msg['To'] = ALERT_EMAIL\n    msg.set_content(body)\n    try:\n        with smtplib.SMTP(SMTP_SERVER, SMTP_PORT) as server:\n            server.starttls()\n            server.login(EMAIL_SENDER, EMAIL_PASSWORD)\n            server.send_message(msg)\n        print(f\"Email alert sent: {subject}\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Email alert failed: {e}\")\n\ndef send_push_alert(title, message):\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(PUSH_API_URL, json={'title': title, 'message': message})\n        print(f\"Push alert sent: {resp.status_code}\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Push alert failed: {e}\")\n\n# ---------------- WEB DASHBOARD ----------------\napp = Flask(__name__)\nsocketio = SocketIO(app)\n\nalert_queue = deque(maxlen=10)\nframe_buffer = deque(maxlen=1)\n\n@app.route('/')\ndef index():\n    return render_template('dashboard.html')\n\n@app.route('/alerts')\ndef get_alerts():\n    return jsonify(list(alert_queue))\n\ndef gen_frames():\n    while True:\n        if frame_buffer:\n            frame = frame_buffer[-1]\n            ret, buffer = cv2.imencode('.jpg', frame)\n            frame_bytes = buffer.tobytes()\n            yield (b'--frame\\r\\n'\n                   b'Content-Type: image/jpeg\\r\\n\\r\\n' + frame_bytes + b'\\r\\n')\n        time.sleep(1/FPS)\n\n@app.route('/video_feed')\ndef video_feed():\n    return Response(gen_frames(), mimetype='multipart/x-mixed-replace; boundary=frame')\n\n# ---------------- MAIN INFERENCE LOOP ----------------\ndef surveillance_loop():\n    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(RTSP_URL)\n    tracker = SimpleTracker()\n    frame_idx = 0\n    alert_sent_ids = set()\n    performance = {'frames': 0, 'detections': 0, 'alerts': 0, 'start': time.time()}\n    # Get the camera FPS (fallback to 25 if not available)\n    cam_fps = cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FPS)\n    if cam_fps <= 0 or cam_fps > 120:\n        cam_fps = 25\n    frame_skip = max(1, int(cam_fps // FPS))\n Reconnecting...\")\n            cap.release()\n            time.sleep(2)\n            cap = cv2.VideoCapture(RTSP_URL)\n            continue\n        frame_idx += 1\n        if frame_idx % frame_skip    performance['frames'] += 1\n        performance['detections'] += len(detections)\n        tracks = tracker.update(detections, frame_idx)\n        # Draw tracks\n        for tid, tr in %H:%M:%S')})\n                send_email_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                send_push_alert(\"Loitering Alert\", msg)\n                socketio.emit('alert', {'type': 'loitering', 'id': 0.7, (0,0,255), 2)\n        for tid in erratic_ids:\n            if tid not in alert_sent_ids:\n                c = tracks[tid]['centroids'][-1]\n                msg = f\"Erratic movement detected for       send_push_alert(\"Erratic Movement Alert\", msg)\n                socketio.emit('alert', {'type': 'erratic', 'id': tid, 'msg': msg})\n                alert_sent_ids.add(tid)\n     prev_centroid = track['centroids'][-1]\n            if len(centroids) > 0:\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n                min_idx = UTILS ----------------\nclass SimpleTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks people by centroid and assigns IDs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, max_lost=30):\n        self.next_id = 0\n        self.tracks = dict()  # id: {'centroids': deque, 'last_seen': frame_idx}\n        self.max_lost = max_lost\n\n    def update(self, detections, frame_idx):\n        \"\"\"detections: list of (x1, y1, x2, y2)\"\"\"\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(centroids - prev_centroid, axis=1)\n                min_idx = np.argmin(distances)\n                if distances[min_idx] < 50:  # Threshold\n 100\n        for i in range(20):\n            if i % 2 == 0:\n                x += 10\n            else:\n                y += 10\n            centroids.append([x, y])\n        tracks = {tid: {'centroids': centroids}}\n        result = detect_erratic(tracks)\n        self.assertIn(tid, result)\n\n    def test_erratic_not_detected_for_straight_movement(self):\n        tid = 2\n
